Shanghai Wins Championship in International Basketball Men's Tournament

Defeated the United States 42-27 last night

Jews defeated Korea 41-36

The Shanghai International Basketball Championship, which was rumored for a while, saw the Chinese and American teams defeat Korea, Jews, Portugal, etc., and met in the morning after last night to compete for this year's championship. As a result, China defeated the United States 42-29 and won this year's championship. The excellence of the performance and the fierceness of the competition between the two teams can be said to be unprecedented. The solid formation, beautiful connection, and rapid movements of the Chinese team, as well as the bravery of Lu Zhongen, were applauded and praised by more than a thousand spectators. Another group, Jews defeated Korea, 41 to 36. Captain Lu's Hard Work and High Achievement

Lu Zhongen, the captain of the Chinese team, commanded the whole team and was concerned in every way, which can be said to be meticulous. He also monitored Shi Guiya, so that Shi had no chance to connect. As a result, the strength of the United States was reduced and they could not use their skills. Lu observed where the emptiness was, and immediately rushed to help, repeatedly seeing miraculous achievements. He scored more than 20 points alone, which was not easy. The amount of scoring is not enough to discuss heroes, but Lu's performance is excellent, and the four words "outstanding talent" are worthy of him. Hard work and high achievement are commendable. Members of the Chinese Team Connect with Each Other

Among the whole team, center He Tong and left forward Liang Guoquan were slightly weak. When he came on the court, He was quite brave, but in the end, he was weakened by lack of strength. Right forward Wei Haiqing showed great skill and was invaluable. He also monitored the opponent's defender Sullivan, so that Sullivan had no chance to carry out secret operations. Defender Li Baojun moved like a rabbit and was as quiet as a virgin. He deserved to be an old general on the battlefield and monitored Smith without leaving an inch. Therefore, Smith's score was very low. The United States relied on Smith's accurate throwing of the basket. Yesterday, after being supervised by Li, he was unable to do anything. The American Team Lacked Throwing Opportunities

On the American team's side, because the two brave generals, Shi Guiya and Smith, were closely guarded by Lu Zhongen and Li Baojun of our team, the American team lost its center of gravity. Center Hannes was also entangled by A Liang. The defenders Euler and Sullivan were no less brave than before, but because our team had good connections, ran through left and right, and were extremely difficult to block, there were gaps everywhere. In addition, Sullivan had few opportunities to throw the basket, and Euler's distant throw was inaccurate, so he made few achievements. The most obvious point between the two sides was the opportunity to throw the basket. The United States lacked the opportunity to throw the basket under the basket, and the Chinese team gradually won. There were very few long shots. From this point, we can know that the Chinese team's precautions were strict and the formation was wonderful, which was better than the American team. The Final Result Was a Difference of 13 Points

The overall situation was that our team was indeed better than the American team. The maximum difference in scores in the first half was 9 to 2. Our team only lagged behind twice with 9 to 11 and 12 to 13. The score in the first half was 16 to 15, and our team won by one point. In the second half, the United States only won the first time with 18 to 16. After that, the score became farther and farther apart. The maximum difference in the middle was 31 to 21 and 38 to 25. The final result was still a difference of 13 points. Taking the Initiative Gave Us an Advantage

When the two teams took the field, our team launched a fierce attack, like a hungry tiger pouncing on a sheep, using excellent passing. Lu Zhongen scored first. In a short time, He Tong also hit a ball, taking the lead with 4 to 0. Seeing that the situation was not good, the American team quickly caught up. Shi Guiya hit a ball. After that, our team's momentum increased, He Tong added another ball, Lu Zhongen made a free throw, and then Wei Haiqing also got a ball. The score Luo took the lead with 9 to 2. Taking the initiative, the momentum was like a broken bamboo. The cheers of the audience were deafening. The Difference in the First Half Was Only One Point

The American team suffered this setback, so they suspended the time to reduce our team's vigor and plan countermeasures and offensive methods. It didn't take long for our team's momentum to increase again. Lu Zhong made 18 to 18. In addition to Lu throwing a ball, he also made two consecutive free throws, adding four points at once. The American team was stimulated, and from then on, it fell apart. The momentum of our team became even stronger. Working Hard to Fight for the Championship

Salute Report

At 9:00 AM on the 15th, the weather cleared, the northwest wind was very strong, there was sand and dust in the sky, the venue was mobilized, and the athletes from various schools gathered in front of the command platform. Chairman Chen Hexuan (1) The whole body stood in awe and faced the center of the playground (2) The Boy Scouts raised the flag, (3) Bowed three times to the party national flag and the Prime Minister's portrait, (4) The chairman respectfully read the Prime Minister's will (5) The chairman's report briefly said that today's weather is very good. In addition to preparing to participate in the National Games, the purpose of our conference is to seek health. "Health" is a sound physical education. "Kang" is to have full physical fitness. The mission we bear is to build China, and it is the health of the majority of the people in the country that can succeed, not the victory of a few people. Therefore, in addition to swimming, all other sports in this sports meeting have everything, and a health competition has been added. It is to use scientific methods to test the degree of health of each participating player, and hope that we will pay attention to physical education at all times in the future. We live in this world of struggle. Without a healthy body, we will not be able to contribute to the society, the country and the world. I hope everyone will work together.

Zhu Jingnong's Speech Then Secretary Zhu Jingnong of the Education Department gave a speech, briefly saying that physical education is for health, and health is for fulfilling the obligations of the people to the country. Let's take a look at how the German youth are doing with physical education now. Germany used to be a country with military education. They are now restricted by the allied countries and cannot have military training opportunities. Their general youth usually pay special attention to personal physical training. Therefore, the result is not only not regressing compared to the past, but the national people's ability to endure hardship is several times more powerful than before. Not only men but also women can gather 50,000 young women in one place to practice gymnastics. Can our Chinese youth be as good as them? Not only are they not as good as Germany, but they are probably not as good as Japan. How dangerous is this, gentlemen? Today's participation in this conference, please do not forget the good example of German youth.

Zhang Daofan's Speech The second Zhang Daofan's speech, briefly said, everyone, are we not shouldering the Prime Minister's will to seek freedom and equality for China? Have we achieved it now? How can we defeat imperialism if we are physically weak and lifeless? Not only can we not carry a gun, but we can't even walk. How can we talk about being better than Germany? I want everyone to take the initiative to promote it, and don't start practicing when the conference is held. Jiangsu is a province with a developed culture. If we promote sports, we can maintain the permanent health of the culture.

Yang Xingfu's Speech The second Yang Xingfu's speech, briefly said, we want to talk about freedom and equality to the outside world, but we must first talk about our own body being free and equal. Our body is weaker than others, which means that our body cannot be equal. Now we have feet that cannot move and hands that cannot lift. We cannot command our own five senses, which means that our body is not free. Gentlemen, if you want freedom and equality for China, please first seek physical education to seek the freedom and equality of your own body. Not only that, but in addition to paying attention to physical education, there is also moral education and group education, which must be obtained in physical education. Where can the moral education and group education in physical education be found? It is found from the meaning of not being afraid of death. The physical education of a nation that is afraid of death is only superficial. Gentlemen, I don't hope that you will get the first, second or third place today. I want you to run to the end one by one. Don't give up halfway when you see that the first, second and third places are not available. If you see that the wind is not right, turn your head and go down. Sports are not for prizes. The purpose of sports is to be sports for the sake of sports and revolution for the sake of revolution.

He Yushu's Speech The second He Yushu's speech, briefly said, Jiangsu is a province with a developed culture, and now it is the province where the capital is located. If it can show its martial spirit, it will not be reduced to the discussion of being weak in literature. Therefore, not only can we not give up our unique history, but we must also promote and express the spirit of sports and be the advocate for all provinces. Meeting Minutes of the Rationality and Education Joint Association 140

The Shanghai Rationality and Education Joint Association held a regular meeting yesterday, chaired by Zhang Yichen. Formalities were observed. A. Report Items (omitted). B. Discussion Items: (1) Regarding the submission of the Association's Notice No. 7 to the Ministry of Interior for record, it was resolved to be handled by the Documentation Department. (2) Regarding the Social Bureau's Fourth Section wanting to change its seal, it was resolved to notify all public offices for their information. (3) Regarding the Nantong Tongshan Hall Public Office being reorganized and established and requesting the dispatch of personnel for guidance, it was resolved to provide written guidance through the Documentation Department. (4) Regarding the Jiangsu Linze Fushan Hall requesting protection, it was resolved to investigate before further review. (5) Regarding the Jiangsu Dongtai Zhishan Hall Public Office sending a letter requesting the organization of a county joint association there, it was resolved to reply by letter and include a copy of the county joint association's charter. (6) Regarding the Shandong Guan County Jingke Hall Public Office wanting to join the association, it was resolved to temporarily register it. (7) Regarding the Henan Shangqiu County Yi Shan Hall Public Office inquiring about membership fees, it was resolved to reply by letter stating that joining the Rationality Society does not require payment of fees. (8) Regarding the Anhui Shou County Zhiwu Hall Public Office requesting to join the association, it was resolved to handle it together with case number six. (9) Regarding the Rationality and Education Model Public Office recommending Comrade Zhang Yichen as a representative, it was discussed and passed. Other cases were omitted.

Children from Kyoto Sent Back by Japan 141

Our consulate-general in Yokohama, Japan, recently telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating, "There is a child, a native of Kyoto, who was stranded in Japan. Now he has been handed over to the Japanese mail ship for repatriation. Please forward a telegram to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for care and repatriation to his hometown." It is reported that the Ministry has telegraphed the Shanghai Office to forward the message to the Public Security Bureau for investigation and handling.

Recent News from the World Moral Society 142

Mr. Cen Yunjie has agreed to take on the position of General President of the World Moral Society. He replied to Mr. Xu Yabo yesterday, stating, "Recently, Mr. Yu Botao brought your esteemed letter. I have read it and learned of the noble aspirations of you gentlemen to save the world with painstaking effort and to promote morality and peace, which I deeply admire. Although I, an old and foolish man, am being drawn into this small endeavor and invited to be your comrade as the General President, I am deeply ashamed and apprehensive upon hearing this order. Considering your earnest expectations and Mr. Yu's account of various matters, how dare I refuse such instruction due to my own inadequacy? I will strive to follow your guidance and await the arrival of more virtuous individuals."

German Doctor Hoffmann to Visit Japan via Shanghai 143

The renowned German medical scientist Dr. Hoffmann, at the invitation of the Japanese Medical Association, will pass through Shanghai within days en route to Osaka to attend the Japan National Medical Congress from April 1st to 5th. It is said that he will make a brief stay in Shanghai during this transit.

Huangdu Native Association Established 144

The Huangdu Shanghai Native Association held a dinner last night at Wanyun Restaurant on Fourth Road to announce its official establishment. Over a hundred people attended, including Xia Langyun and Zhao Shutong. The association's charter was passed, officers were elected, and it was decided that the Phoenix Inn on Tianjin Road would serve as the association's location. Many people joined, and there are plans to extensively solicit members and expand the organization. It is said that a major officers' meeting is planned for next Wednesday to discuss important matters.

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Recruiting Clerks 145

The Municipal Health Bureau is recruiting a clerk familiar with official documents. The examination will be held at 9:00 AM on the 18th of this month at the Bureau's location in Maojia Lane, Nanshi. The qualifications are said to be: age between 20 and 40, experience in handling official documents in government agencies, pure character, and meticulous and diligent work. The examination subjects are drafting official documents, summarizing reports, and managing archives. After being hired, there will be a one-month trial period to determine whether to retain the candidate. A guarantor is also required. The salary is 35 yuan per month, and outstanding performance may lead to salary increases or promotions.

Memorial Service for Mrs. Zhong Ketuo Today 146

At 3:00 PM on March 16th, the Central Opium Prohibition Committee and five other organizations will hold a memorial service at St. Peter's Church in Shanghai for Mrs. Zhong Ketuo (née Tu Huiqin). During her lifetime, Mrs. Zhong devoted herself to social work and spared no effort, so Chinese and Westerners alike feel sorrow for her passing. It is expected that many people will attend to pay their respects.

Obituary of the Xie Family 147

Madam Hong, the mother of Ningbo merchant Xie Jiliang, passed away on November 21st of last year. Recently (on the 13th), Mr. Xie's wife, Madam Xu, also passed away due to illness. Madam Xu had two sons, the elder named Shiwen, who works at the Shanghai Maritime Insurance Company, and the younger named Shiyan, who works in the business department of this newspaper. Madam Xu had three grandchildren (both grandsons and granddaughters), and both she and her mother-in-law, Madam Hong, were very virtuous. The two coffins are temporarily placed in the South Factory of the Shangming Cemetery.

News from Various Labor Unions 148

Postal Workers' Union: The 20th Executive Committee meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Zhu Xuefan. (1) Formalities were observed. (2) Chairman's report (omitted). (3) Discussion items: (A) Regarding the proposed revision of the salary scale for postal assistants and below, the union had previously submitted a proposal to the authorities for review, but it has not yet been implemented. Currently, there is a high demand in various regions to improve the treatment of postal assistants. To avoid disputes, how should this be proceeded with? (Resolution) (i) Report to the All-China Postal Workers' Union and request them to order all regions to imitate the Union's request to unify steps. (ii) Actively negotiate with the authorities. (B) How should item number eight of the report items be handled? (Resolution) Approve the Economic Department to allocate funds from the special expenses and order the department to submit invoices and equipment lists. (C) How should item number six of the report items be handled? (Resolution) Reply that the request violates the public pension regulations and cannot be approved. (D) How should item number seven of the report items be handled? (Resolution) Reply that the request will be handled together with the pending case of improving the treatment of messengers. (E) How should item number five of the report items be handled? (Resolution) The original submission should be forwarded to the Post Office Headquarters for review. (F) How should items number four and nine of the report items be handled? (Resolution) The Secretariat should send a separate reply. (G) The Second Branch proposed that messengers (errand runners) and letter carriers with 15 years of service should be given preferential examination procedures, as resolved by the union council. Please expedite negotiations with the authorities. (Resolution) Continue to handle it as a pending case. (H) The Land Committee proposed that the union continue to negotiate with the authorities regarding in-house letter carriers. (Resolution) Instruct the Negotiation Department to continue negotiating. (4) Adjournment.

Commercial Press General Affairs Department Workers' Union: On the afternoon of March 11th, a general meeting was held to elect the seventh session of executive committee members and supervisory committee members. A total of 180 members attended. Yang Weiyin, Wan Pusheng, and Zheng Zheng were elected as the presidium, and Chen Shuzhi and Tang Xiaoceng were the recorders. Zhang Gunfu reported on the union's previous affairs and finances. Wan Pusheng, Mu Gengxun, Yu Shuzhou, Zhao Zengqi, Chen Shuzhi, Shan Qihan, Zhang Ruyu, Yang Weiyin, and Chen Longzhang were elected as the nine executive committee members. Zhu Shou Kang, Wang Weiwu, Jin Rongtai, and Wu Dujun were elected as the four alternate executive committee members. Li Jimin, Bian Ziqiang, and Cheng Hengcai were elected as the three supervisory committee members, and Zhang Gunfu and Zheng Zheng were elected as the two alternate supervisory committee members. On the morning of the 13th, a continued meeting was held, and under the supervision of the Party representative, they took the oath of office. Yesterday, the Union's Executive and Supervisory Committees held a temporary meeting, chaired by Wan Pusheng, and Wan Pusheng, Yu Shuzhou, and Zhang Ruyu were mutually elected as the standing committee members of the Executive Committee, and Cheng Hengcai was elected as the chairman of the Supervisory Committee.

China Merchants Bureau Wharf Workers' Union: The 22nd Executive Committee regular meeting was held yesterday, with Dan Xishou publicly elected as chairman. (A) Report Items (omitted). (B) Discussion Items: (1) Regarding the Social Bureau filling out worker death investigation forms, it was resolved that after the Mutual Aid Committee fills out the forms, the Executive Committee will handle them. (2) Regarding the Huazhan Branch Executive Committee reporting the promotions of Yang Yixu, Sun Shousong, Shen Zongrui, and Lou Jiacai, it was resolved to send a letter to the manager of Huazhan to promote them according to the regulations. (3) Regarding the Nanzhan Branch Executive Committee reporting and requesting the Bureau to subsidize rice expenses, it was resolved to send a letter to the Bureau. (4) Regarding the Nanzhan Branch Executive Committee reporting that five out of the many goods loaded were red clay, it was resolved to file it with the Nanzhan Executive Committee. A temporary motion was made regarding the failure to issue February salaries to date, and a resolution was passed to demand payment. At 9:00 AM on the 17th (i.e., Monday), all Executive Committee members will go to the Bureau to demand payment.

Wing On Factory Workers' Union: An emergency meeting was convened yesterday, chaired by Jin Yaowen. Discussion items: (1) Regarding the Union's Standing Executive Committee members Yan Gunian, Wang Yuncheng, Jin (name missing), and Secretary Chen Hanjian, who were temporarily suspended from their positions by the Municipal Party Department due to being responsible for reporting the Tan Huanxiang bribery case, and now that the case has concluded, it was resolved to submit a request to the Municipal Party Department to reinstate them and to the Social Bureau to reinstate Comrades Wang and Yan to their factory jobs. (2) Regarding the wages for the holiday on the anniversary of the death of the General Manager of this term, should a letter be sent to the capital side requesting payment? It was resolved to first send Standing Committee member Jin Yaowen to negotiate with the capital side. (3) Regarding the funds borrowed from the Eighth District Party Department during the Union's preparation period, which they have now sent a letter requesting repayment, how should this be handled? It was resolved to send a letter to the Eighth District Party Department requesting an extension of the repayment period. (4) Regarding the discovery of reactionary leaflets outside the Wing On Factory repair shop and the men's restroom entrance, how should this be handled? It was resolved to report it to the Eighth District Party Department for handling. The meeting was adjourned after the discussions.

Lüye Workers' Union: The 11th Executive Committee meeting was held yesterday, chaired by Zhang Yaowu. Formalities were observed. Discussion: (1) Should the Union hold regular meetings of executive officers to discuss progress? Please review and decide. Resolution: Reserved. (2) Should the Union re-draft the survey form and conduct another survey? Please review and decide if it is appropriate. Resolution: Passed. (3) Should a letter be sent to the capital-side industry association, stating that they should not obstruct the survey work? Please review and decide. Resolution: Passed. (4) Should responsible personnel be designated for the survey work? Please vote. Resolution: Zhu Yuanshun was elected as the director. (5) Regarding proposing to revise the treatment conditions, should we first negotiate with the capital side? Should responsible representatives be designated? Please review and decide if it is appropriate. Resolution: Song Yao Woqing, Pan Rongting, Zhang Dejin, Dai Jiajie, Zhu Yuanshun, Liang Tikang, Ni Tinglu, Xiong Kunshan, and Zhang Yaowu were elected as the responsible representatives. (6) Should the Economic Management Committee designate a chairman to assume full responsibility? Please review and decide. Resolution: Dong Xiqing was elected as the chairman. (7) Announcement to Workers: Resolution: Comrade Xu Zhongming was assigned to draft it. (8) Adjournment.

Zhabei Sanitation Workers' Union, Hongkou Branch Reorganization Executive Committee: The 5th meeting was held yesterday, chaired by Zhang Qinglu. Discussion items: (1) Zhou Buqing submitted the names of Song Qichang and Zhou Kexin, requesting to join the Union as members, and said that they are already working within the Union's scope. How should this be handled? Resolution: (A) Report to the higher level to stop it. (B) Investigate the reason for the two people's work. (C) If any members of the Union are found to have committed fraud, report it to the higher level for strict handling. (2) Xu Xuechen and others requested that the eight new manure carts that they had made be allowed to start working on April 1st, as Mr. Qin Boyan of the Municipal General Labor Union had approved. Resolution: Report to the General Labor Union. (3) Xu Xuechen and nine others requested that the members' congress elect executive officers, opposing the representative system. Resolution: Permission is granted to hold a members' congress. (4) The former Executive Committee refused to hand over. Resolution: Submit to the Congress. (5) Omitted. (6) Should unemployed members be investigated? Resolution: Please Zhu Shousheng and Li Hua handle it. (7) Date of the Inaugural Meeting: Resolution: (A) Set for 1:00 PM on the 26th of this month. (B) Report to the higher level. (8) If Xie Zhengchang comes to cause trouble on the day of the Congress, how should this be handled? Resolution: Notify and stop it. (9) Congress venue: Resolution: The Union Hall. (10) If manure carts are broken and leak, affecting sanitation, and the police station imposes penalties, how should this be handled? Resolution: Send a letter to the capital-side requesting them to replace the carts with new ones; otherwise, if the police station imposes penalties, the capital-side should be responsible.

Huayang Printing Workers' Union: The 52nd Executive Committee meeting was held the day before yesterday, chaired by Xia Hailin. The meeting opened as usual. Discussion items: (1) The Social Bureau issued a notice for questioning regarding the conditions. Appointed Qu Shoukang and Wang Xingquan as the two representatives to be responsible for the reply. (2) The capital side of the Huawei Branch did not give double pay. Reported to the Social Bureau. (3) A worker from the Oriental Branch was dismissed by the capital side without reason. Requested the Social Bureau to mediate. (4) The Shanghai Public Bus Workers' Union intends to default on the meeting venue subsidy. How should this be handled? Resolution: Send personnel again to pursue the responsible person of the Union. Otherwise, notify all sectors to declare disassociation. (5) Standing Committee member Yin Wenbai resigned. Unanimously retained.

Zhejiang Ning Slaughtering Duck Workers' Union: A joint meeting of the executive groups was held yesterday, chaired by Jiang Liangcai. Discussion items: (1) The Union's financial expenditure is insufficient and exceeds the budget. How should this be handled? (Resolution) Sublease the remaining rooms, cancel the teahouse, passed. (2) Workers refuse to pay monthly dues. (Resolution) Report to the General Labor Union for handling. (3) Appointed Jiang Liangcai, Fang Chang, and Yang Qiu Zengxian to collect monthly dues. Weather Report 149

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The weather is clear and cold. There is a cyclone over the Sea of Japan. The entire national coastline has north winds, with occasional fog in some areas. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 57.9 degrees and the lowest was 38.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 68.5 degrees and the lowest was 31.9 degrees.

Acknowledgment: Thank you for the Commercial Press's gift of the 11th issue of the 15th volume of the Women's Magazine yesterday.

Letter to the Editor

I recently read a news article in your newspaper's local news section titled "Shanghai Tea Workers' Union: Tea Worker Drunk and Gnaws on Finger." After investigation, our Standing Committee member Hong Zhonghe was injured yesterday while trying to mediate, and the incident is indeed true. However, it was not our Union that held the election for executive and supervisory congress at the Xingjiang Dunzhitang Hall, but rather the Xingjiang Dunzhitang Hall itself held the election for executive and supervisory committee members. However, Standing Committee member Hong Zhonghe was our Union's representative and attended the meeting. Now the report says that the Shanghai Tea Workers' Union held the election for the executive and supervisory committees at the Xingjiang Dunzhitang Hall, which is likely a misunderstanding. I hereby request a correction. Respectfully, Shanghai Tea Workers' Union, March 15th.
